class="Card__Content__Kicker"><ul class="SectionLabelWrapper"></ul></div><h3 class="Card__Content__Heading">National Geographic’s nonprofit work</h3><div class="Card__Content__Dek"><p>National Geographic Society funds the best and brightest individuals dedicated to scientific discovery, exploration, education and storytelling to illuminate and protect the wonder of our world. National Geographic Explorers are continuing to push the boundaries of knowledge, uncovering new insights about the natural and cultural worlds, and strengthening our connection to them and one
